  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_40fde4e7-7144-490f-8cad-8aec881b7e03'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer11300310587775266108">When Ellery moved to New York with her boyfriend, she thought they’d live happily ever after in their small New York apartment.   <span id="freeText11300310587775266108" style="display:none">When Ellery moved to New York with her boyfriend, she thought they’d live happily ever after in their small New York apartment. She never thought he’d pack his bags and leave because he “needed space.” With her newfound single status and fear of being alone, Ellery buries herself in her artwork and paintings until one night she helps a mysterious intoxicated stranger get home safely. Little did she know the mysterious stranger is none other than CEO and millionaire Connor Black. After finding Ellery in his kitchen the next morning and assuming she broke his #1 rule about sleepovers, he becomes intrigued, not only by her stubbornness and defiance, but by her kindness.<br /><br />Connor Black, emotionally dead and damaged, that stemmed from a personal tragedy, made a vow to never love or fall in love with a woman, until Ellery Lane walked into his life by accident. After she opens up and shows him her world, Connor starts to feel emotions and feelings he never knew existed. Despite the rumors and warnings regarding Connor Black and his use and misuse of women, Ellery finds herself being drawn into his world. <br /><br />Ellery knows they can never be together because she is harboring a deep secret that could destroy Connor emotionally forever. <br /><br />Join Connor and Ellery as they embark on a journey of courage, love and strength. Will it be enough to save them?</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525172853?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525172853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12101088735597726537"><blockquote>
  <i>Do you remember watching Sweet November?<br/><br/>The way Sarah wanted to live her life as though every moment were her last?<br/><br/>The way Nelson couldn't bear to see her fade?</i>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407952i/797411.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/><br/>So let's just suppose we have this young woman. <b>Ellery.</b> Who has experienced more pain that should be allowed for a 23-year-old person. To whom fate keeps shoving even more dirt. Which thankfully she can take. Because she met this man. <b>Connor.</b> Whose emotional vulnerability has been locked down a long time now. Who seems </span>
  <span id="freeText12101088735597726537" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>Do you remember watching Sweet November?<br><br>The way Sarah wanted to live her life as though every moment were her last?<br><br>The way Nelson couldn't bear to see her fade?</i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407952i/797411.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>So let's just suppose we have this young woman. <b>Ellery.</b> Who has experienced more pain that should be allowed for a 23-year-old person. To whom fate keeps shoving even more dirt. Which thankfully she can take. Because she met this man. <b>Connor.</b> Whose emotional vulnerability has been locked down a long time now. Who seems detached from feeling, sensing, trully living due to something that scarred his past and him along with it. <br><br>But she breaks through to him and he's able to learn from her..<br><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407952i/797412.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>“Infinity is forever, and that is what you are to me, you are my forever Mr. Black.”<br>He kissed my lips, “There's no limit to what I wouldn't do for you. Just ask and it will be done, no matter the sacrifice.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>The path is not easy. No person that has to deal with this kind of faith and strength tests can do so without that support. Confrontations are inevitable, and thankfully the drama was not pushed over the top but instead, it was kept to the reality and seriousness of the situation. <br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I laughed, “I’m already sick, what’s the difference?”<br>He stared down at me with a strange look on his face and did something I never thought Connor Black would do. He laid down beside me and looked up at the sky. I looked over at him as he struggled to keep his eyes open as the rain pelted him in the face; a small smile crossed my lips.<br>“Why are you doing this?” he asked as he turned and looked at me.<br>“Cause I can lay here and no one will know I’m crying.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>And in the end of the day, they are each other's rock. They ground and heal each other. And that's exactly what they did.<br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He softly took a hold of both my wrists and looked at them, rubbing the tattoos lightly. I saw the<br>anguish in his eyes.<br>“I noticed these at the hospital when you were receiving chemo. I’ve been waiting for you to show me; why Ellery?” He asked.<br>I rolled over as the morphine settled through my body and I was able to step out of bed and slowly walked over to the window. “Because at some point you have to realize that some people can stay in your heart, but not in your life, and this is my way of keeping you in my heart.”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407952i/797413.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>“I was simply a man with no meaning until I met you and I’m proud of whom I’ve become because of you. We have been through a lot together and we will<br>continue to go through a lot, but we’ll conquer whatever life throws our way. I want to thank you for being my best friend and my lover.”<br>Suddenly he got down on one knee and pulled a small velvet box from his pocket. The tears wouldn’t stop flowing down my face. “I want to be more than just<br>your lover, I want to be your happily ever after, your best friend, your husband and I want you for my wife; will you marry me Ellery Lane?”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407952ra/797414.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>“I could never understand my purpose in this world. I have had nothing but pain and loss my whole life. But now I know why god saved me the first time. It was<br>so I could find you. Then he saved me the second time so I could love you forever. This house is perfect; you are perfect and no one will ever take that away from us.<br>Our love is infinite and I’m going to spend the rest of my life showing you.”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407952i/797415.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>“She’s like her beautiful mother and she’s going to be a fighter. I can’t wait to see her and hold her in my arms,” he whispered.<br>I smiled as I interlaced our fingers, “I can’t either. She’s the reason god saved me a third time. She’s our little miracle.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4149515546081033325">It always saddens me when I have the privilege of an ARC of a much anticipated release from a debut author. I really, really wanted to love this but sadly, it just didn't work for me.<br/><br/>The story is great although I did have a hard time understanding the character's motivations even when it was explained to me but I struggled with the writing style, especially the lack of contractions which made the narrative kind of stilted for me which stopped me fully connecting and there's also a distinct lack </span>
  <span id="freeText4149515546081033325" style="display:none">It always saddens me when I have the privilege of an ARC of a much anticipated release from a debut author. I really, really wanted to love this but sadly, it just didn't work for me.<br /><br />The story is great although I did have a hard time understanding the character's motivations even when it was explained to me but I struggled with the writing style, especially the lack of contractions which made the narrative kind of stilted for me which stopped me fully connecting and there's also a distinct lack of punctuation. I also found the misuse of the word 'to' instead of 'too' really difficult to cope with.<br /><br />I know this will work for some - I'm just so very sorry that it really didn't work for me.<br /><br />2.5 stars<br /></span>

<div id="review_518881875" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/518881875" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/518881875?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer518881875" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10307080840439579850">Let me start off by saying that I really enjoyed this story. I liked how Connor and Ellery met and I just plain liked how Ellery did her own thing and didn't bow down to anyone. <br/><br/>That being said, there is a lot going on in and maybe even a bit too much. Also, while usually spelling and grammar don't usually bother me, I had a hard time with a few things in this book. 'To' versus 'too' and the lack of contractions interrupted the flow of the story for me but <i>in no way</i> would I consider DNF'ing. <br/><br/>Ell</span>
  <span id="freeText10307080840439579850" style="display:none">Let me start off by saying that I really enjoyed this story. I liked how Connor and Ellery met and I just plain liked how Ellery did her own thing and didn't bow down to anyone. <br><br>That being said, there is a lot going on in and maybe even a bit too much. Also, while usually spelling and grammar don't usually bother me, I had a hard time with a few things in this book. 'To' versus 'too' and the lack of contractions interrupted the flow of the story for me but <i>in no way</i> would I consider DNF'ing. <br><br>Ellery was refreshing and surprising because at first, I thought she was just going to be another needy girl. She had been with her boyfriend for four years and not really been on her own, so she was upset when they broke up but I'm glad she snapped out of it. I loved all the interactions with Connor while they were 'friends'. How she made him eat a hot dog and pizza with his fingers and eat ice cream!! How she didn't let him order her around. <br><br>Connor started off as a jerk....well, he has a few other jerk-worthy moments but then you get to know him and understand why. I liked that Ellery brought out another side of him and I loved that he was there for Ellery even when she said she didn't want him to be. <br><br>Ellery and Connor were great together but boy, could they fight! Like Denny said, they are both really stubborn! It was hard because instead of talking things out, they would take off. Connor is used to getting his way but he has also had some things happen to him that has caused him to close himself off. Ellery has had a rough life and it's caused her to not allow other people to treat her badly. It leads to some interesting moments and maybe some that were a little over the top. <br><br>There is a lot of drama. Both Connor and Ellery have things and people in their pasts that they haven't been honest about. It was really great seeing them try to work things out. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786977i/489916.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I loved Peyton....she was a really great best friend to Ellery. I liked how she would help set things straight with Ellery and like she said, that's what best friends are for. <br><br>The paintings that Ellery did added a special touch to the story especially a certain one that was included in the epilogue. I was a surprised that she wasn't upset at what happened with the first three paintings. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794088i/586983._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>The epilogue made me really happy. It was a win-win-win. I found out that SL is writing the next book and it will be Connor's POV...I can't wait!! <br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ "Would you be interested in being a companion?"<br><br>♥ “You are different Ellery, and you scare me. You make me feel things I never have before. You’re all I think about day and night. I feel empty inside when you’re not around. Don’t you understand? It isn’t supposed to be this way, and if I sleep with you this will all be ruined.”<br><br>♥ “Infinity is forever, and that is what you are to me, you are my forever Mr. Black.”<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786977i/489917._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>♥ “I love you, not only for who you are, but for the person I have become because of you. This is my forever to you.”</span>
  <a data-text-id="10307080840439579850" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_539447860" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/539447860" />
    <a title="Stella" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15739800-stella"><img alt="Stella" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587151711p2/15739800.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539447860?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stella" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stella" href="/user/show/15739800-stella">Stella</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15739800-stella?shelf=billionaire-powerfullmen">billionaire-powerfullmen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15739800-stella?shelf=good-message">good-message</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15739800-stella?shelf=standalones">standalones</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539447860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11693387019459523110">*Spoiler Alert*<br/>Oh I loved the first few chapters of this book and thought I had finally found my BOOK OF THE MONTH (February) but it turned out to be a real disappointment. I'm really sad to say that, but I'd be lying if I said any differently. I'm not even going to mention the editing/writing issues. I was really disappointed in it being so CLICHÉ and the amount of death, suicide and DEAD people contained in this story.<br/>A famous writer once said that if you are writing a ROMANCE and you feel the</span>
  <span id="freeText11693387019459523110" style="display:none">*Spoiler Alert*<br />Oh I loved the first few chapters of this book and thought I had finally found my BOOK OF THE MONTH (February) but it turned out to be a real disappointment. I'm really sad to say that, but I'd be lying if I said any differently. I'm not even going to mention the editing/writing issues. I was really disappointed in it being so CLICHÉ and the amount of death, suicide and DEAD people contained in this story.<br />A famous writer once said that if you are writing a ROMANCE and you feel the need to 'kill' MORE than 4 people for the sake of the plot, you are doing it WRONG. Well, we have 6 or 7 'dead' people if you don't include the ALMOST dead heroine. Why would you need 7 dead people and two pairs of Twins? Yup, same here. No clue.<br />I found CONNOR a really interesting character, it's plain to see that if his character had been more developed and more focused on his RELATIONSHIP with Ellie (rather than in her HEALTH CONDITION) this story would have been much, WAY more interesting. But, unfortunately, the focus was the HEALTH CONDITION. A total bummer.<br />Ellie started witty and fun, ended up egotistical and whiny.<br />I don't mean to sound heartless, I think her condition was very sad and I am sure lots of people will relate to her 'state', but I still don't understand why SO MUCH drama. (Isn't one character on deathbed enough?). Geez... <br />Anyways, I could go on and on here but I know lots of better REVIEWS are being written by MUCH BETTER REVIEWERS about the same 'issues' so I rather stop here.<br />Of course It had a few good moments, but from 75% on I just wanted this story to end...<br />Will I read other books from this author, Why not? I just hope the next books have fewer dead people and more LOVE and focus on the characters and their relationship.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11693387019459523110" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_545342842" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/545342842" />
    <a title="Wicked Nyx" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14259375-wicked-nyx"><img alt="Wicked Nyx" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1358209147p2/14259375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/545342842?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wicked Nyx" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wicked Nyx" href="/user/show/14259375-wicked-nyx">Wicked Nyx</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14259375-wicked-nyx?shelf=xbattle-of-the-books">xbattle-of-the-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14259375-wicked-nyx?shelf=borrowed">borrowed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14259375-wicked-nyx?shelf=xbotb-march-2013">xbotb-march-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer545342842" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16849851529272626351">1 ½ Stars<br/><br/>Oh I so WANTED to like this book. That being said, I didn’t, I couldn’t. And yet I couldn’t stop reading it…it was like watching a car crash, I just couldn’t look away.<br/><br/>The first third of the book, I spent half of my time being jarred out of the story by the strange lack of contractions. The book is written in first person POV and even the inner dialogue was strangely bereft of contractions. How many people sound so utterly formal all the time, not only when speaking, but also when think</span>
  <span id="freeText16849851529272626351" style="display:none">1 ½ Stars<br /><br />Oh I so WANTED to like this book. That being said, I didn’t, I couldn’t. And yet I couldn’t stop reading it…it was like watching a car crash, I just couldn’t look away.<br /><br />The first third of the book, I spent half of my time being jarred out of the story by the strange lack of contractions. The book is written in first person POV and even the inner dialogue was strangely bereft of contractions. How many people sound so utterly formal all the time, not only when speaking, but also when thinking?<br /><br />Speaking of POV, the entire book is from Ellery’s POV, except for one strange, short chapter written from Connor’s POV. We learn nothing about his motivations or his inner self and it seems to serve no purpose in the story arc.<br /><br />Every time they have a fight it turns into the sacking of Carthage, including the razing of the city and the salting of the earth. No small disagreements, just global thermonuclear war followed by one or both of them leaving. And then with very little growth or development, magically they get back together and are having sex.<br /><br />And speaking of the sex, this was a very un-erotic book of erotica. The following excerpts are from a single two-page section:<br /><br /><i><br />He gently inserted his finger in me and feeling the wetness before inserting another. I gasped at the pleasure and arched my back for him to go deeper. His tongue ran circles around my swollen area forcing me to release my pleasure to him<br /><br />********<br /><br />He sat up and moved fluently in and out of me. He reached his hands around and grabbed my breasts, squeezing them and pinching each nipple before moving his hand down and rubbing my aching spot.<br /></i><br /><br />(That’s right people, he moved <b>fluently</b> in and out of her.) All their sex scenes are like this - short, barely descriptive and supremely UN-sexy. And you can also see the profound lack of good comma usage. I would rather have too many commas than the extreme dearth of commas that this book presents to the reader. I found myself having to read sentences several times in order to get the right meaning.<br /><br />I think the author might also be unaware of the use of the apostrophe in order to show possession - instead of Connor's plane, it is Connors plane; instead of Connor's penthouse, it is Connors penthouse...I don't know if I saw a single correctly used apostrophe to show possession in the entire book.<br /><br />I gave this 1 ½ star because the storyline had promise, and I did finish the book. I am unbelievably happy that I borrowed this book and didn’t spend any money on it.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16849851529272626351" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_539411091" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/539411091" />
    <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite"><img alt="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368215503p2/3758447.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539411091?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite">Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=bad-boy-hero">bad-boy-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=commitment-issues">commitment-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=serious-issues">serious-issues</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539411091" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16993240286696362360">This was an ok read for me. <br/><br/>I liked a lot about Ellery. She was spunky and sarcastic and didn't let anyone push her around. I liked Connor too, most of the time,but I never felt like we actually got to know him. I liked how their relationship started. I enjoyed<br/>that they were friends first. I didn't understand Ellery managing to fall in love with Connor when she knew basically zero about him (since he basically shared zero about himself with her until much later in the book)<br/><br/>I saw the twist coming</span>
  <span id="freeText16993240286696362360" style="display:none">This was an ok read for me. <br /><br />I liked a lot about Ellery. She was spunky and sarcastic and didn't let anyone push her around. I liked Connor too, most of the time,but I never felt like we actually got to know him. I liked how their relationship started. I enjoyed<br />that they were friends first. I didn't understand Ellery managing to fall in love with Connor when she knew basically zero about him (since he basically shared zero about himself with her until much later in the book)<br /><br />I saw the twist coming. I was seriously irritated with Connor's reaction. He did a couple of things, usually when they were fighting, that just ticked me off. Maybe if I felt like I knew him better, it wouldn't have bothered me so much, but it did. <br /><br />I hated the way they fought. When something happened, it was a huge explosion, and they both went for the jugular. I was particularly unexcited the time he called her a bitch and a slut. It drove me insane that she always ran away when things got tough (and I hated that he let her sometimes). They just seemed really really dysfunctional. Now, this would not have bothered me so much, except it is never resolved, After each dramatic blowup, they come back together, but nothing is ever discussed or resolved - so not shockingly, it happens again (and again). <br /><br />This is why I couldn't even get really excited by the ending. Once again, their issues are never really addressed, and we should just be happy with the (rushed) HEA. <br /><br />Oh, and one other thing <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[. What was up with the psychic aunt and her knowing that Ellery was sick. Could there not have been a more normal way for it to come out? And what was with him being with the twin sister of the chick that killed herself. It just seemed insanely out if character.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />Overall, ok. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16993240286696362360" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/541257507?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer541257507" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12643330330976290612">I know I am in the minority here but this did not do it for me at all. First off, I found the writing a bit stilted... there was no flow to it - some of the sentences had words like "do not" instead of "don't" . This may seem like nit-picking but if I am paying for a books I am expecting something. There seemed to be too much going on here. Maybe I have had my fill of billionaires, taking charge, younger woman who is less well off than the hero. Yep, think my days of YA and NA books are over. al</span>
  <span id="freeText12643330330976290612" style="display:none">I know I am in the minority here but this did not do it for me at all. First off, I found the writing a bit stilted... there was no flow to it - some of the sentences had words like "do not" instead of "don't" . This may seem like nit-picking but if I am paying for a books I am expecting something. There seemed to be too much going on here. Maybe I have had my fill of billionaires, taking charge, younger woman who is less well off than the hero. Yep, think my days of YA and NA books are over. although some might argue that this is not necessarily a NA book but I am 47 and if the heroine is only in early twenties that is NA for me. The heroine was just too emotional, going from one extreme to the other - OK, she had a lot to be emotional about. And the Aunt and her proclamations. Sorry - hate to put a downer on a first time author but I feel I have to give an honest opinion. I think sometimes I am too caught up in all the five stars some books get and feel I HAVE TO read them.</span>

<div id="review_542455771" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/542455771" />
    <a title="Crista" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3194546-crista"><img alt="Crista" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1284946251p2/3194546.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/542455771?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Crista" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Crista" href="/user/show/3194546-crista">Crista</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=tear-jerkers">tear-jerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=hot">hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=tortured-heroes">tortured-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=tortured-heroines">tortured-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer542455771" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15595017547764559657">Original Review posted at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com'>www.sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com</a><br/><br/><br/>Whew! This one really got to me and I'm glad I had a tissue box handy while reading.<br/><br/>Forever Black again goes "back to the well" and features a multi-millionare hero. Connor is CEO of his own company, sexy as all get out, and has commitment issues. Sound familiar? Well, don't be too quick to judge, as that is where the similarities to so much of what is out there....ends.<br/><br/>I loved so many things about this book. First and foremost, Eller</span>
  <span id="freeText15595017547764559657" style="display:none">Original Review posted at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com">www.sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com</a><br /><br /><br />Whew! This one really got to me and I'm glad I had a tissue box handy while reading.<br /><br />Forever Black again goes "back to the well" and features a multi-millionare hero. Connor is CEO of his own company, sexy as all get out, and has commitment issues. Sound familiar? Well, don't be too quick to judge, as that is where the similarities to so much of what is out there....ends.<br /><br />I loved so many things about this book. First and foremost, Ellery and Connor are great friends before they become lovers. This slow developing relationship feels natural and "right". They are in some ways very opposite, and Elle teaches Connor a lot about what it means to live. She's an artist and a free spirit compared to Connor's more serious and rule following ways. She challenges him in such fun ways, and watching a man who only uses women for pleasure begin to truly care for a woman gave me all sorts of warm fuzzies. The friendship between these characters was amazing.<br /><br />This book is a tearjerker. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Elle is sick with recurrent cancer <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. The complexity and challenges that this relationship face because of this fact sets this book apart from all the rest. The emotions, reactions, and conflict involving Elle's health felt very real to me. I appreciated where both characters were coming from and the resulting internal turmoil they experienced.<br /><br />Elle and Connor are strong characters. They stand up for themselves and what they believe in. Some reviewers have mentioned that their arguments became bothersome, but for me, their arguments added to the authenticity of the relationship. I believed in this couple. <br /><br />This is a spicy book with no kink. Connor is straight vanilla with no BDSM tendencies.<br /><br />The story is told in first person from Elle's viewpoint, except for one chapter that without warning switches to Connor's POV. I have to admit that this was a bit strange. Some may be bothered by the editing, but it wasn't bad enough to affect my enjoyment or my recommendation.<br /><br />Overall, just a very lovely and believable story of a "meant to be" couple.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15595017547764559657" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText16715128561704140965" style="display:none"><b> 4 – 4.5 STARS </b> <br /><br />I was looking for an emotional romance and a HEA… Well well, that is exactly what I was looking for and got. <br /><br />I really enjoyed the book. Was a quick read. <br /><br />When I started, I thought OMG here we go again, a BILLIONAIRE. When I hear that word these days I actually cringe. Possessive / Rude / Sex sex sex (ok that part I never moan about haha) <br /><br />But this story was actually very good, they didn’t have sex almost until 50% into the book. This book was very emotional. Ellery’s story was very sad and what she had to go through in her 24years. Both had their demons to over come. (I don’t want to give away to much of the story you will have to read the book yourself ☺ hie hie) <br /><br />The epilogue was sweet and happy that they had a HEA. <br /><br /><b> <u> FAVOURITE QUOTES / LINES </u></b>  <br /><br /><i> “What the fuck is this man’s problem. <div id="review_2052154041" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2052154041" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45826136-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523893682p2/45826136.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2052154041?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/45826136-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2052154041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2553617488804260220">This is a really horrible book. Bad writing - the author does not know the difference between "to" and "too". It had stilted dialogue which attempted to be proper but just seemed unnatural. It manipulates the reader, and honest to God I find it disgusting the author just uses shit like this as a plot device without handling it wth sensitivity:<br/><br/>The heroine's mother had cancer and died when she was a kid. The heroine had cancer at 16. The heroine attempted suicide by slashing her wrists to prevent </span>
  <span id="freeText2553617488804260220" style="display:none">This is a really horrible book. Bad writing - the author does not know the difference between "to" and "too". It had stilted dialogue which attempted to be proper but just seemed unnatural. It manipulates the reader, and honest to God I find it disgusting the author just uses shit like this as a plot device without handling it wth sensitivity:<br /><br />The heroine's mother had cancer and died when she was a kid. The heroine had cancer at 16. The heroine attempted suicide by slashing her wrists to prevent her father the pain from having to her die from cancer (cause suicide is somehow better right?). She got the treatment, got better, but dun dun dun, her alcoholic daddy who ignored her after her mother died because he was so in love with her died too when she was 18. Shes 23 and volunteers in the soup kitchen for the homeless, has a bucket list of things she wants to do because she embraces life, and hides from everyone that she has cancer again and is refusing treatment. And once she meets the hero, her surrogate parents (aunt and uncle) die in a car crash, but she like gets over it; the funeral was actually used as a scene for her to hear people talking about her, she bursts and shows them her wrist scars, and stages a huge attention seeking drama llama scene by not actually mourning their deaths and somehow making it about her.<br /><br />The author needs to recognise, you can deal with one of these issues and create a brilliant story. <br /><br />But don't worry, with the exclusion of her new hit reappearing cancer, the heroine vomits her life story to anyone and everyone who will listen: the hero on their first date, his driver, her apartment manager when she plane hops to California and has just met the guy for barely five minutes.<br /><br />On the night she meets the hero, who is smashed and she sees get slapped by a woman, she decides I'm going to take this guy home and "accidentally" falls asleep at his place nvm he could be some rapist and she wants to be a good Samaritan. <br /><br />The hero is a millionaire (shocker) and finds her when she tells him her name. They forge some weird friendship where she shits out her tragic lifestory and the geezer tells her nothing because you know "privacy" (some people don't tell their live stories after a couple of minutes). He's ha: easy access sexual relationships in the past. She runs away, she comes back, he chases her, he rejects her, she runs away, he insults her, they finish but rekindle. It's a toxic juvenile relationship where they don't discuss anything and are so stupid. She's in the middle of her cancer treatment (like they aren't expecting her tomorrow?) when they have a fight and she plane hops to California because mysteriously she's found a clinical trial to join (its leukaemia - a common cancer; why would they want to accept her? Clinical trials are selective but whatever, we've established the author isn't too smart a cookie). They have fights one minute where he resents her and her cancer and how he can't do his work because he's looking after her, shouts at her insensitively for not telling him, abandons her, randomly reappears, then she sees him with multiple women, he calls HER a slut for the way she dresses, she throws a vase at him (and I can't condone violence just cos she's a woman, that's wrong, if a man did that, "domestic abuse"), she goes from wanting to live happily with him to never wanting to see him again - moving from his penthouse to her box flat to going to another state, then she finds out he had a vasectomy, and plays her woe is me card about how she wouldn't be a good mother anyway and has crap genes etc etc. And THEN she learns he has a dead ex gf who committed suicide at 18 and only recently was he in a contractual relationship actually fucking the twin sister because apparently she manipulated him and he felt he needed to make amends (the woman who slapped him at the club when she first saw him) until recently because the woman wants to be exclusive. And he gets hit on frequently and never shuts it down, just enjoys it and the heroine gets violent with the women, name calls, slut shames and punches them, when your man shouldn't be engaging but you know, this story is dumb so. The epilogue featured a kid and he reversed his vasectomy (when only a couple chapters ago he confided he never wanted kids) and her clinical trial miraculously cured her. I'm done. <br /><br />I can't even explain anymore but this story is pure bs.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2553617488804260220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Georgia Cruz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8816126-georgia-cruz"><img alt="Georgia Cruz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454052223p2/8816126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/541350768?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia Cruz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia Cruz" href="/user/show/8816126-georgia-cruz">Georgia Cruz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=swoonfest-overload">swoonfest-overload</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=best-book-ever">best-book-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=best-of-best-books-ever">best-of-best-books-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8816126-georgia-cruz?shelf=will-forever-haunt-me">will-forever-haunt-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer541350768" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14539080891509475815"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I could never understand my purpose in this world. I have had nothing but pain and loss my whole life. But now I know why god saved me the first time. It was so I could find you. Then he saved me the second time so I could love you forever”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><a href='http://s144.beta.photobucket.com/user/suyen02chubby/media/tumblr_lyby0bnki11qdlh0d_zps09b33fb3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410454ra/804800.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_lyby0bnki11qdlh0d_zps09b33fb3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>This was beautifully written! <br/>Even though I've seen many similar stories like this one, it still amazed me how Love truly conquers all. 'Beautiful' is not enough to express how AMAZING this story is.</b><br/><br/>I watched in awe on how Connor Black and Ell</span>
  <span id="freeText14539080891509475815" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I could never understand my purpose in this world. I have had nothing but pain and loss my whole life. But now I know why god saved me the first time. It was so I could find you. Then he saved me the second time so I could love you forever”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s144.beta.photobucket.com/user/suyen02chubby/media/tumblr_lyby0bnki11qdlh0d_zps09b33fb3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410454ra/804800.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lyby0bnki11qdlh0d_zps09b33fb3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>This was beautifully written! <br>Even though I've seen many similar stories like this one, it still amazed me how Love truly conquers all. 'Beautiful' is not enough to express how AMAZING this story is.</b><br><br>I watched in awe on how Connor Black and Ellery Lane took every step of the way to always be together forever. I loved this book so much that I spend a lot of time sniffing, wiping tears, gushing, swooning, and basically floating for Connor's ability to melt every single women with a pulse. <br><br><i>
  <b>“Infinity is forever, and that is what you are to me, you are my forever Mr. Black.”</b>
</i><br><br>Their constant words for each other is what keeps me from grabbing a tissue because I always end up crying for this stubborn couple who love each other so much. It's a heart-warming story. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Because at some point you have to realize that some people can stay in your heart, but not in your life, and this is my way of keeping you in my heart.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s144.beta.photobucket.com/user/suyen02chubby/media/tumblr_midraiDnEo1ribltno1_400_large_zpsd06e9583.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText13812276476607428917" style="display:none">This is my first book by Sandi Lynn. I do not know what to expect from it. Based on many good ratings in Goodreads, I took a dive. <br /><br />The story is about a young woman, Ellery who, at one night, helped a drunken stranger in the bar. And that stranger is a billionaire Connor Black. They strikes up a friendship and turns into love relationship. <br />I did not expect that I love these 2 characters interact. Their sweet, sweet humble banter is so.... delicious sweet. Like a tiramisu cake. I smile and cheering for them when they finally get their act together and get their HEA. <br /><br />I wish that Miss Lynn can hire a better editor. Some of her wording, especially the sexy steamy scene is awkward and stiff. So I can not really feel the depth of their emotional connection in bed. <br /><br />Overal I like this book. I will read another book by this author. <br /><br />4 Infinity stars. </span>

  <span id="freeText14919553138063177375" style="display:none">I’m gonna have to give this one 3.5 stars. An emotional and enjoyable read for me.<br><br>Meet <b> Mr. Connor Black</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/ccbf5314-2525-49fd-9f50-4c08688d2595_zps9b25f152.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409835i/802848.jpg" alt=" photo ccbf5314-2525-49fd-9f50-4c08688d2595_zps9b25f152.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>“What’s to tell, I’m a 30 year old CEO, I have more money than I will ever need; I don not do relationships; I usually get everything I want, and I do whatever I want.”</b><br><br>and <b>Ellery Lane </b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/8fe4122e-4576-460d-993f-08c83c12c34c_zps22cb0471.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409835i/802849.jpg" alt=" photo 8fe4122e-4576-460d-993f-08c83c12c34c_zps22cb0471.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>‘Nothing lasts forever.’</b><br><br>The way Elle and Connor met was a little unconventional. Elle’s boyfriend of four years had just left her, so her best friend Peyton dragged her out to a club. She see’s Connor there, and he is falling down, stumbling, completely shit faced. She decides to be a good samaritan and take him home. She gets a cab and goes to settle him in his fantastic home. Connor didn’t really know what was going on or why Elle was there... he thought it was for a much different reason.<br><b>
  <i>“You are a beautiful woman and I am going to fuck you really hard.”</i>
</b><br>Okay, that part had me cracking up. Elle and Connor become friends. They start to develop feelings for each other, but Connor is the typical rich, dominate, I don’t do relationship types. But he has never felt like this with anyone else. <br><b>
  <i>“You are different Ellery, and you scare me. You make me feel things I never have before. You’re all I think about day and night. I feel empty inside when you’re not around.”</i>
</b><br><br>Their relationship has drama. Lots and lots of drama. Elle has a secret. When Connor finally finds out, he kind of freaks. But he makes it up to her. They fight a lot and make up a lot, they just have those types of personalities. <br><b>
  <i>“You two are the most stubborn people on the face of this earth and you couldn’t be more perfect for each other.”</i>
</b><br>Eventually, they get it together though. I enjoyed the ending, even though it was a little rushed, it was sweet. <br><br>Will I ever get sick of reading about dominate, rich, hot guys... NO! I really did like Connor. There was just a little too much drama for me. Still, I liked this one. I wanted to love it, but it took me a while to connect with the story and characters. It was enjoyable for me and I still feel like it was a worthy debut novel! <br><br><b>
  <i>“I could never understand my purpose in this world. I have had nothing but pain and loss my whole life. But now I know why god saved me the first time. It was so I could find you. Then he saved me the second time so I could love you forever.”</i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/7d301fc1-0fd5-4568-a2be-462953dacd0f_zpsc9bed977.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409835i/802850.jpg" alt=" photo 7d301fc1-0fd5-4568-a2be-462953dacd0f_zpsc9bed977.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Some of my favorite quotes... <br><br><i>“Because at some point you have to realize that some people can stay in your heart, but not in your life, and this is my way of keeping you in my heart.”<br><br>“You make me feel alive like no one ever has.”<br><br>“Memories are our way of holding onto the things we love, and I plan on making the most beautiful memories with you.”<br><br>“I love you, not only for who you are, but the person I have become because of you. This is my forever to you.”<br><br>“I’ve never loved anyone like I love you and no matter what we’ve been through or are going to go through, that will never change.”<br><br>“You have filled the void in my heart and soul that I never knew existed until you weren’t by my side.”</i></span>

  <span id="freeText12409312755258820459" style="display:none">I've struggled a bit with the review for this one.. I really liked the "idea" of the story. I also liked the 1st half of the book. Connor and Ellery had good chemistry starting out but at some point I just felt like their connection was lost not far after the midway point. This story had such potential to be really really good.. I never felt the sympathy I needed to feel for Ellery and her illnes, I hated the way she handled it, then I seriously didnt like the way Connor handled it then once they got back to being there for each other it just seemed forced. I just couldnt connect.. I'll definilty give Sandi Lynn another try with her next book.. because this one did have lots of potential..               <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2579092-jennifer?shelf=books-i-want-to-re-read">books-i-want-to-re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2579092-jennifer?shelf=extremely-rich-hero">extremely-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2579092-jennifer?shelf=hea">hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2579092-jennifer?shelf=tearjerker">tearjerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2579092-jennifer?shelf=2013-release-date">2013-release-date</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522706900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12560357990268069172">This book was spectacular in my opinion. I was a little nervous to read this because I thought it was going to be so much like all the other Billionaire love stories out there already. I must say I was pleasantly surprised this book was so different. Yes it had the mega rich man that was slightly broken with and issue from his past and it had the young woman who was also broken in many ways, but this story was just so much more then that. This book wasn't just a couple who argued and had make up</span>
  <span id="freeText12560357990268069172" style="display:none">This book was spectacular in my opinion. I was a little nervous to read this because I thought it was going to be so much like all the other Billionaire love stories out there already. I must say I was pleasantly surprised this book was so different. Yes it had the mega rich man that was slightly broken with and issue from his past and it had the young woman who was also broken in many ways, but this story was just so much more then that. This book wasn't just a couple who argued and had make up sex all the time there was actually another storyline that played into this book. Now don't get me wrong there was arguing and hot make up sex but it didn't revolve around that. I have to say I fell in love with Connor, he ranks right up there with Christian, Gideon and Travis for me. He was a douche in the beginning but as time went on he totally melted my heart. I loved loved loved Ellery. She was one of the strongest heroines I have read about in a long time. We definitely need more leading ladies like her in books. I loved how she didn't take crap from anyone especially Connor. Connor was very dominant but she didn't cower and hide, she stood up to him and told him off when need be. Ellery has seen and been through her fair share of pain in her short life, but she still persevered and came out stronger in the end. I was a little aggravated with her towards the end because she was such a strong woman, that strength sometimes turned into stubbornness and some of the drama at the end of the book could have been avoided. I will say that I enjoyed the mix of story to sex scenes....this book wasn't overpowered by one or the other it had a great mix. I also loved the secondary characters .... Peyton, Ellery's BFF, was awesome. She was funny and strong also, but she was a great support for Ellery when she needed it. <br /><br />As I have said before that what makes a great book, is what emotions I feel throughout the book....This book evoked many different emotions from me, I was laughing, crying, yelling, and just over all loving. That to me deserves 5 stars. I would definitely recommend this book to everyone.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12560357990268069172" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer530134907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7111802111771877812">First of all, I LOVED this book. I read it in one sitting and thought about it all day afterwards.<br/><br/>I originally gave this four stars and after pondering it changed my mind and gave it a full five stars. Here is why:<br/><br/>First of all I loved the characters, but I also wanted to slap the s**t out of them! The angst between these two was absolutely brutal. But it's like that horrible scene in a movie where you know it's going to rip your heart out and you just can't look away.<br/><br/>There is a huge spoiler that</span>
  <span id="freeText7111802111771877812" style="display:none">First of all, I LOVED this book. I read it in one sitting and thought about it all day afterwards.<br /><br />I originally gave this four stars and after pondering it changed my mind and gave it a full five stars. Here is why:<br /><br />First of all I loved the characters, but I also wanted to slap the s**t out of them! The angst between these two was absolutely brutal. But it's like that horrible scene in a movie where you know it's going to rip your heart out and you just can't look away.<br /><br />There is a huge spoiler that I won't include here because I know you will click on it. I always click on the spoilers. Let me just tell you this. It's heart wrenching. It makes you look at your life and say...wow...the hard decisions in my life suddenly seem like childs play compared to this. <br /><br />It starts out with Connor being a player who doesn't date woman, but meets Ellery and is entranced by her for some reason. That seems typical enough, but let me tell you. It's not. Ellery has a huge secret that could completely break Connor's new found love for her.<br /><br />Never fear these two do find their HEA and it is a beautiful one. However, this is where I had my 4 star 5star dilemma. At first I felt like the ending was too abrubt. The whole book was angst and turmoil and heartbreak and then all of a sudden, BAM they're together and everything works out perfectly. <br /><br />At first I was like, that's it? After practically giving me PTSD with this book, it works out-just like that? And then I started thinking about it more. Sometimes, more often then not actually, things happen quickly. They hit you fast and unexpected. That is how Ellery and Connor fell in love and that is how they ended. So really, the ending makes perfect sense.<br /><br />Great job Sandi!! I can't wait to read more from you!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17426260912002332538">I don't like to write bad things about a book because I can't imagine how difficult it must be write a book but this one really pissed me off. Besides the amount of unnecessary drama, the annoying insta-love (if you can even call it love) and the boring interaction between the characters.<br/>There's something that bother me the most and i can't forgive and it was how jerk Connor Black is. He's an obsessive, control maniac who thinks that because of his "tragic past" he's allowed to treat women like </span>
  <span id="freeText17426260912002332538" style="display:none">I don't like to write bad things about a book because I can't imagine how difficult it must be write a book but this one really pissed me off. Besides the amount of unnecessary drama, the annoying insta-love (if you can even call it love) and the boring interaction between the characters.<br />There's something that bother me the most and i can't forgive and it was how jerk Connor Black is. He's an obsessive, control maniac who thinks that because of his "tragic past" he's allowed to treat women like objects and being a total douchebag. He literally says to Ellery that she's a slut for how she was dressing like and that if she gets raped it's her fault because she was asking for it. When i read it i was like "that's it, i'm done with this garbage" but i only finish it because there was like 10 pages left and let me tell you that that happy ending it's just absurd.<br />In conclusion, i lost my whole time. No offense but i've read fanfictions from a teenager that are better than this book.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11456302029075511121"><b>**3.5 Stars**</b><br/><br/>The main reason why this story got 3.5 stars from me is because I found it addictive. I couldn't put it down and whenever I got the chance I picked up my iPhone to finish reading it. However, I found a lot of errors which bothered me and were distracting from the story. I also wanted to smack Elle's character, she was so flip floppy and unnecessarily annoying and difficult. I did enjoy Connor's character though! Although, for how long the book was I felt like their relationship rush</span>
  <span id="freeText11456302029075511121" style="display:none"><b>**3.5 Stars**</b><br /><br />The main reason why this story got 3.5 stars from me is because I found it addictive. I couldn't put it down and whenever I got the chance I picked up my iPhone to finish reading it. However, I found a lot of errors which bothered me and were distracting from the story. I also wanted to smack Elle's character, she was so flip floppy and unnecessarily annoying and difficult. I did enjoy Connor's character though! Although, for how long the book was I felt like their relationship rushed and there wasn't a strong build up. And don't get me started on the last 5-7 chapters, such randomness and fluff that dragged on for no reason.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1gurH7VQ47d6V3v3Ue/2TdZoxBypeNPHdbSlYu/ASy5iBSWRDmYIBhCxtB363gG4wMNiAtkuJfokBWm0CMbZNA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9xXPX9P7Tu5TJTFZnSljuqL1Yz6NO+OGa402K9DCHtpDG0HRaM2lXznD/rM2GJRPtF7FIP1tFbs6PPr9N8SMwA==')})
  }

Non avrebbe mai immaginato che lui avrebbe fatto i bagagli e se ne sarebbe andato perché aveva “bisogno di spazio”. Così da un giorno all’altro Ellery si è ritrovata single e, per combattere la solitudine, si è rifugiata nella sua arte e nei suoi dipinti. Un incontro fortuito però cambia tutto: una notte Ellery aiuta un ubriaco a tornare a casa sano e salvo. Non sa che il misterioso sconosciuto in realtà è il milionario Connor Black. Quando, il mattino dopo, Connor trova Ellery nella sua cucina, pensa che quella ragazza abbia violato la regola numero uno: nessuna può restare a dormire dopo essere stata a letto con lui. Vorrebbe mandarla via, ma, suo malgrado, si sente attratto dalla sua ostinazione, dalla sua aria di sfida, dalla sua dolcezza… Una storia d’amore e di coraggio che ha appassionato le lettrici, raccontata secondo il punto di vista di Ellery e di Connor, nella quale la passione è travolgente e i colpi di scena e i batticuori non mancano mai.La trilogia bestseller del New York Times, di USA Today e del Wall Street JournalI giudizi delle lettrici:«Un libro sorprendente. Pacchetto completo: ho riso e sorriso un sacco, ho pianto e soprattutto mi sono innamorata di Ellery e Connor.»JoJo«Scritto meravigliosamente!
